I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[Bug]: Regression in alpha config upstreams with regex (+rewrite target)
### OAuth2-Proxy Version

7.6.0

### Provider

google

### Expected Behaviour

In 7.5.1 we were running the following upstreamConfig

```
      upstreamConfig:
        upstreams:
          - id: app
            path: ^/(.*)$
            rewriteTarget: /$1
            proxyWebSockets: true
            uri: http://app:3000
          - id: api
            path: ^/api(/stripe/webhook|/graphql|/downloads)(.*)$
            rewriteTarget: /api$1$2
            proxyWebSockets: true
            uri: http://api:5555
```

Where all our requests went to the app except a few prefixed by /api/graphql for example.

### Current Behaviour

Upgrading to 7.6.0, this no longer works. All requests to the app end up returning the html served on / (in our example the base html from NextJS, but all js/css/etc also returns that base html) In a similar fashion, all things accessing the api component return the /api endpoint on the /api route.

I've tried with httpbin to see if is was on our side, but also here it can only serve / and not any other routes.

The output in the logs is the same as in 7.5.1

![CleanShot 2024-02-15 at 11 27 44@2x](https://github.com/oauth2-proxy/oauth2-proxy/assets/16780/c44778ee-80a5-4737-9e9a-05f66fff091f)

In this screenshot both / and /spec.js return the contents of /

I saw some more logger calls in the go code but i'm unsure on how to get these printed out.

- Changing the container version to 7.5.1 and all works again as it should
- the -alpine container of 7.6.0 has the same issue, so it is not the image itself
- I've scanned all commits that went into 7.6.0 but cannot find any change that is related, my guess is that it might have been one of the dependency updates

### Steps To Reproduce

1. helm install the 7.5.1 version
2. configure the upstreams like above
3. WORKS
4. upgrade the helm chart (image goes to 7.6.0
5. ERROR
6. change just the image version of the deployment to 7.5.1
7. WORKS

### Possible Solutions

_No response_

### Configuration details or additional information

_No response_

    16	// newRewritePath creates a new middleware that will rewrite the request URI
    17	// path before handing the request to the next server.
    18	func newRewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, writer pagewriter.Writer) alice.Constructor {
    19	        return func(next http.Handler) http.Handler {
    20	                return rewritePath(rewriteRegExp, rewriteTarget, writer, next)
    21	        }
    22	}
    23	
    24	// rewritePath uses the regexp to rewrite the request URI based on the provided
    25	// rewriteTarget.
    26	func rewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, writer pagewriter.Writer, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
    27	        return http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
    28	                reqURL, err := url.ParseRequestURI(req.RequestURI)
    29	                if err != nil {
    30	                        logger.Errorf("could not parse request URI: %v", err)
    31	                        writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
    32	                                Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
    33	                                RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
    34	                                AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse request URI: %v", err),
    35	                        })
    36	                        return
    37	                }
    38	
    39	                // Use the regex to rewrite the request path before proxying to the upstream.
    40	                newURI := rewriteRegExp.ReplaceAllString(reqURL.Path, rewriteTarget)
    41	                reqURL.Path, reqURL.RawQuery, err = splitPathAndQuery(reqURL.Query(), newURI)
    42	                if err != nil {
    43	                        logger.Errorf("could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err)
    44	                        writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
    45	                                Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
    46	                                RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
    47	                                AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err),
    48	                        })
    49	                        return
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                req.RequestURI = reqURL.String()
    53	                req.URL.Path = reqURL.Path // set path for websocket connections
    54	                next.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
    55	        })
    56	}
    57	
    58	// splitPathAndQuery splits the rewritten path into the URL Path and the URL
    59	// raw query. Any rewritten query values are appended to the original query
    60	// values.
    61	// This relies on the underlying URL library to encode the query string.
    62	// For duplicate values it appends each as a separate value, e.g. ?foo=bar&foo=baz.
    63	func splitPathAndQuery(originalQuery url.Values, raw string) (string, string, error) {
    64	        s := strings.SplitN(raw, "?", 2)
    65	        if len(s) == 1 {
    66	                return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        queryValues, err := url.ParseQuery(s[1])
    70	        if err != nil {
    71	                return "", "", nil
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        for key, values := range queryValues {
    75	                for _, value := range values {
    76	                        originalQuery.Add(key, value)
    77	                }
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
    81	}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/reproduce_issue.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"net/url"
	"regexp"
	"strings"

	"github.com/justinas/alice"
)

// Mock objects to satisfy the rewritePath interface
type MockWriter struct{}
func (m *MockWriter) WriteErrorPage(rw http.ResponseWriter, opts interface{}) {}

// Copying relevant parts from rewrite.go for reproduction
func rewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
	return http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
		reqURL, err := url.ParseRequestURI(req.RequestURI)
		if err != nil {
			panic(err)
		}

		// Use the regex to rewrite the request path before proxying to the upstream.
		newURI := rewriteRegExp.ReplaceAllString(reqURL.Path, rewriteTarget)
		reqURL.Path, reqURL.RawQuery, err = splitPathAndQuery(reqURL.Query(), newURI)
		if err != nil {
			panic(err)
		}

		req.RequestURI = reqURL.String()
		req.URL.Path = reqURL.Path // set path for websocket connections
		next.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
	})
}

func splitPathAndQuery(originalQuery url.Values, raw string) (string, string, error) {
	s := strings.SplitN(raw, "?", 2)
	if len(s) == 1 {
		return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
	}

	queryValues, err := url.ParseQuery(s[1])
	if err != nil {
		return "", "", nil
	}

	for key, values := range queryValues {
		for _, value := range values {
			originalQuery.Add(key, value)
		}
	}

	return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
}

func main() {
	// Replicating the reported issue
	// id: app
	// path: ^/(.*)$
	// rewriteTarget: /$1
	
	re := regexp.MustCompile("^/(.*)$")
	target := "/$1"
	
	testCases := []string{
		"/",
		"/spec.js",
		"/static/css/main.css",
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		req := httptest.NewRequest("GET", tc, nil)
		handler := rewritePath(re, target, http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
			fmt.Printf("Original: %s, Rewritten RequestURI: %s, Rewritten Path: %s\n", tc, r.RequestURI, r.URL.Path)
		}))
		handler.ServeHTTP(httptest.NewRecorder(), req)
	}
}
'

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/reproduce_issue.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"net/url"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

func splitPathAndQuery(originalQuery url.Values, raw string) (string, string, error) {
	s := strings.SplitN(raw, "?", 2)
	if len(s) == 1 {
		return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
	}

	queryValues, err := url.ParseQuery(s[1])
	if err != nil {
		return "", "", nil
	}

	for key, values := range queryValues {
		for _, value := range values {
			originalQuery.Add(key, value)
		}
	}

	return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
}

func rewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
	return http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
		reqURL, err := url.ParseRequestURI(req.RequestURI)
		if err != nil {
			panic(err)
		}

		// Use the regex to rewrite the request path before proxying to the upstream.
		newURI := rewriteRegExp.ReplaceAllString(reqURL.Path, rewriteTarget)
		reqURL.Path, reqURL.RawQuery, err = splitPathAndQuery(reqURL.Query(), newURI)
		if err != nil {
			panic(err)
		}

		req.RequestURI = reqURL.String()
		req.URL.Path = reqURL.Path // set path for websocket connections
		next.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
	})
}

func main() {
	re := regexp.MustCompile("^/(.*)$")
	target := "/$1"
	
	testCases := []string{
		"/",
		"/spec.js",
		"/static/css/main.css",
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		req := httptest.NewRequest("GET", tc, nil)
		handler := rewritePath(re, target, http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
			fmt.Printf("Original: %s, Rewritten RequestURI: %s, Rewritten Path: %s\n", tc, r.RequestURI, r.URL.Path)
		}))
		handler.ServeHTTP(httptest.NewRecorder(), req)
	}

	re2 := regexp.MustCompile("^/api(/stripe/webhook|/graphql|/downloads)(.*)$")
	target2 := "/api$1$2"
	testCases2 := []string{
		"/api/graphql",
	}
	for _, tc := range testCases2 {
		req := httptest.NewRequest("GET", tc, nil)
		handler := rewritePath(re2, target2, http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
			fmt.Printf("Original: %s, Rewritten RequestURI: %s, Rewritten Path: %s\n", tc, r.RequestURI, r.URL.Path)
		}))
		handler.ServeHTTP(httptest.NewRecorder(), req)
	}
}
'

    16	// newRewritePath creates a new middleware that will rewrite the request URI
    17	// path before handing the request to the next server.
    18	func newRewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, writer pagewriter.Writer) alice.Constructor {
    19	        return func(next http.Handler) http.Handler {
    20	                return rewritePath(rewriteRegExp, rewriteTarget, writer, next)
    21	        }
    22	}
    23	
    24	// rewritePath uses the regexp to rewrite the request URI based on the provided
    25	// rewriteTarget.
    26	func rewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, writer pagewriter.Writer, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
    27	        return http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
    28	                reqURL, err := url.ParseRequestURI(req.RequestURI)
    29	                if err != nil {
    30	                        logger.Errorf("could not parse request URI: %v", err)
    31	                        writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
    32	                                Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
    33	                                RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
    34	                                AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse request URI: %v", err),
    35	                        })
    36	                        return
    37	                }
    38	
    39	                // Use the regex to rewrite the request path before proxying to the upstream.
    40	                newURI := rewriteRegExp.ReplaceAllString(reqURL.Path, rewriteTarget)
    41	                reqURL.Path, reqURL.RawQuery, err = splitPathAndQuery(reqURL.Query(), newURI)
    42	                if err != nil {
    43	                        logger.Errorf("could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err)
    44	                        writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
    45	                                Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
    46	                                RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
    47	                                AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err),
    48	                        })
    49	                        return
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                req.RequestURI = reqURL.String()
    53	                req.URL.Path = reqURL.Path // set path for websocket connections
    54	                next.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
    55	        })
    56	}
    57	
    58	// splitPathAndQuery splits the rewritten path into the URL Path and the URL
    59	// raw query. Any rewritten query values are appended to the original query
    60	// values.
    61	// This relies on the underlying URL library to encode the query string.
    62	// For duplicate values it appends each as a separate value, e.g. ?foo=bar&foo=baz.
    63	func splitPathAndQuery(originalQuery url.Values, raw string) (string, string, error) {
    64	        s := strings.SplitN(raw, "?", 2)
    65	        if len(s) == 1 {
    66	                return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        queryValues, err := url.ParseQuery(s[1])
    70	        if err != nil {
    71	                return "", "", nil
    72	        }
    73	
    74	        for key, values := range queryValues {
    75	                for _, value := range values {
    76	                        originalQuery.Add(key, value)
    77	                }
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        return s[0], originalQuery.Encode(), nil
    81	}

    20	// HTTP proxies fail to connect to upstream servers.
    21	type ProxyErrorHandler func(http.ResponseWriter, *http.Request, error)
    22	
    23	// NewProxy creates a new multiUpstreamProxy that can serve requests directed to
    24	// multiple upstreams.
    25	func NewProxy(upstreams options.UpstreamConfig, sigData *options.SignatureData, writer pagewriter.Writer) (http.Handler, error) {
    26	        m := &multiUpstreamProxy{
    27	                serveMux: mux.NewRouter(),
    28	        }
    29	
    30	        if upstreams.ProxyRawPath {
    31	                m.serveMux.UseEncodedPath()
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        for _, upstream := range sortByPathLongest(upstreams.Upstreams) {
    35	                if upstream.Static {
    36	                        if err := m.registerStaticResponseHandler(upstream, writer); err != nil {
    37	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not register static upstream %q: %v", upstream.ID, err)
    38	                        }
    39	                        continue
    40	                }
    41	
    42	                u, err := url.Parse(upstream.URI)
    43	                if err != nil {
    44	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("error parsing URI for upstream %q: %w", upstream.ID, err)
    45	                }
    46	                switch u.Scheme {
    47	                case fileScheme:
    48	                        if err := m.registerFileServer(upstream, u, writer); err != nil {
    49	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not register file upstream %q: %v", upstream.ID, err)
    50	                        }
    51	                case httpScheme, httpsScheme, unixScheme:
    52	                        if err := m.registerHTTPUpstreamProxy(upstream, u, sigData, writer); err != nil {
    53	                                return nil, fmt.Errorf("could not register %s upstream %q: %v", u.Scheme, upstream.ID, err)
    54	                        }
    55	                default:
    56	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("unknown scheme for upstream %q: %q", upstream.ID, u.Scheme)
    57	                }
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        registerTrailingSlashHandler(m.serveMux)
    61	        return m, nil
    62	}
    63	
    64	// multiUpstreamProxy will serve requests directed to multiple upstream servers
    65	// registered in the serverMux.
    66	type multiUpstreamProxy struct {
    67	        serveMux *mux.Router
    68	}
    69	
    70	// ServerHTTP handles HTTP requests.
    71	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) ServeHTTP(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
    72	        m.serveMux.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
    73	}
    74	
    75	// registerStaticResponseHandler registers a static response handler with at the given path.
    76	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) registerStaticResponseHandler(upstream options.Upstream, writer pagewriter.Writer) error {
    77	        logger.Printf("mapping path %q => static response %d", upstream.Path, derefStaticCode(upstream.StaticCode))
    78	        return m.registerHandler(upstream, newStaticResponseHandler(upstream.ID, upstream.StaticCode), writer)
    79	}
    80	
    81	// registerFileServer registers a new fileServer based on the configuration given.
    82	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) registerFileServer(upstream options.Upstream, u *url.URL, writer pagewriter.Writer) error {
    83	        logger.Printf("mapping path %q => file system %q", upstream.Path, u.Path)
    84	        return m.registerHandler(upstream, newFileServer(upstream, u.Path), writer)
    85	}
    86	
    87	// registerHTTPUpstreamProxy registers a new httpUpstreamProxy based on the configuration given.
    88	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) registerHTTPUpstreamProxy(upstream options.Upstream, u *url.URL, sigData *options.SignatureData, writer pagewriter.Writer) error {
    89	        logger.Printf("mapping path %q => upstream %q", upstream.Path, upstream.URI)
    90	        return m.registerHandler(upstream, newHTTPUpstreamProxy(upstream, u, sigData, writer.ProxyErrorHandler), writer)
    91	}
    92	
    93	// registerHandler ensures the given handler is regiestered with the serveMux.
    94	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) registerHandler(upstream options.Upstream, handler http.Handler, writer pagewriter.Writer) error {
    95	        if upstream.RewriteTarget == "" {
    96	                m.registerSimpleHandler(upstream.Path, handler)
    97	                return nil
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        return m.registerRewriteHandler(upstream, handler, writer)
   101	}
   102	
   103	// registerSimpleHandler maintains the behaviour of the go standard serveMux
   104	// by ensuring any path with a trailing `/` matches all paths under that prefix.
   105	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) registerSimpleHandler(path string, handler http.Handler) {
   106	        if strings.HasSuffix(path, "/") {
   107	                m.serveMux.PathPrefix(path).Handler(handler)
   108	        } else {
   109	                m.serveMux.Path(path).Handler(handler)
   110	        }
   111	}
   112	
   113	// registerRewriteHandler ensures the handler is registered for all paths
   114	// which match the regex defined in the Path.
   115	// Requests to the handler will have the request path rewritten before the
   116	// request is made to the next handler.
   117	func (m *multiUpstreamProxy) registerRewriteHandler(upstream options.Upstream, handler http.Handler, writer pagewriter.Writer) error {
   118	        rewriteRegExp, err := regexp.Compile(upstream.Path)
   119	        if err != nil {
   120	                return fmt.Errorf("invalid path %q for upstream: %v", upstream.Path, err)
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        rewrite := newRewritePath(rewriteRegExp, upstream.RewriteTarget, writer)
   124	        h := alice.New(rewrite).Then(handler)
   125	        m.serveMux.MatcherFunc(func(req *http.Request, _ *mux.RouteMatch) bool {
   126	                return rewriteRegExp.MatchString(req.URL.Path)
   127	        }).Handler(h)
   128	
   129	        return nil
   130	}
   131	
   132	// registerTrailingSlashHandler creates a new matcher that will check if the
   133	// requested path would match if it had a trailing slash appended.
   134	// If the path matches with a trailing slash, we send back a redirect.
   135	// This allows us to be consistent with the built in go servemux implementation.
   136	func registerTrailingSlashHandler(serveMux *mux.Router) {
   137	        serveMux.MatcherFunc(func(req *http.Request, _ *mux.RouteMatch) bool {
   138	                if strings.HasSuffix(req.URL.Path, "/") {
   139	                        return false
   140	                }
   141	
   142	                // Use a separate RouteMatch so that we can redirect to the path + /.
   143	                // If we pass through the match then the matched backed will be served
   144	                // instead of the redirect handler.
   145	                m := &mux.RouteMatch{}
   146	                slashReq := req.Clone(context.Background())
   147	                slashReq.URL.Path += "/"
   148	                return serveMux.Match(slashReq, m)
   149	        }).Handler(http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
   150	                http.Redirect(rw, req, req.URL.String()+"/", http.StatusMovedPermanently)
   151	        }))
   152	}
   153	
   154	// sortByPathLongest ensures that the upstreams are sorted by longest path.
   155	// If rewrites are involved, a rewrite takes precedence over a non-rewrite.
   156	// When two upstreams define rewrites, whichever has the longest path will take
   157	// precedence (note this is the input to the rewrite logic).
   158	// This does not account for when a rewrite would actually make the path shorter.
   159	// This should maintain the sorting behaviour of the standard go serve mux.
   160	func sortByPathLongest(in []options.Upstream) []options.Upstream {
   161	        sort.Slice(in, func(i, j int) bool {
   162	                iRW := in[i].RewriteTarget
   163	                jRW := in[j].RewriteTarget
   164	
   165	                switch {
   166	                case iRW != "" && jRW != "":
   167	                        // If both have a rewrite target, whichever has the longest pattern
   168	                        // should go first
   169	                        return len(in[i].Path) > len(in[j].Path)
   170	                case iRW != "" && jRW == "":
   171	                        // Only one has rewrite, it goes first
   172	                        return true
   173	                case iRW == "" && jRW != "":
   174	                        // Only one has rewrite, it goes first
   175	                        return false
   176	                default:
   177	                        // Default to longest Path wins
   178	                        return len(in[i].Path) > len(in[j].Path)
   179	                }
   180	        })
   181	        return in
   182	}
   183

    42	// newHTTPUpstreamProxy creates a new httpUpstreamProxy that can serve requests
    43	// to a single upstream host.
    44	func newHTTPUpstreamProxy(upstream options.Upstream, u *url.URL, sigData *options.SignatureData, errorHandler ProxyErrorHandler) http.Handler {
    45	        // Set path to empty so that request paths start at the server root
    46	        // Unix scheme need the path to find the socket
    47	        if u.Scheme != "unix" {
    48	                u.Path = ""
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        // Create a ReverseProxy
    52	        proxy := newReverseProxy(u, upstream, errorHandler)
    53	
    54	        // Set up a WebSocket proxy if required
    55	        var wsProxy http.Handler
    56	        if upstream.ProxyWebSockets == nil || *upstream.ProxyWebSockets {
    57	                wsProxy = newWebSocketReverseProxy(u, upstream.InsecureSkipTLSVerify)
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        var auth hmacauth.HmacAuth
    61	        if sigData != nil {
    62	                auth = hmacauth.NewHmacAuth(sigData.Hash, []byte(sigData.Key), SignatureHeader, SignatureHeaders)
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        return &httpUpstreamProxy{
    66	                upstream:  upstream.ID,
    67	                handler:   proxy,
    68	                wsHandler: wsProxy,
    69	                auth:      auth,
    70	        }
    71	}
    72	
    73	// httpUpstreamProxy represents a single HTTP(S) upstream proxy
    74	type httpUpstreamProxy struct {
    75	        upstream  string
    76	        handler   http.Handler
    77	        wsHandler http.Handler
    78	        auth      hmacauth.HmacAuth
    79	}
    80	
    81	// ServeHTTP proxies requests to the upstream provider while signing the
    82	// request headers
    83	func (h *httpUpstreamProxy) ServeHTTP(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
    84	        scope := middleware.GetRequestScope(req)
    85	        // If scope is nil, this will panic.
    86	        // A scope should always be injected before this handler is called.
    87	        scope.Upstream = h.upstream
    88	
    89	        // TODO (@NickMeves) - Deprecate GAP-Signature & remove GAP-Auth
    90	        if h.auth != nil {
    91	                req.Header.Set("GAP-Auth", rw.Header().Get("GAP-Auth"))
    92	                h.auth.SignRequest(req)
    93	        }
    94	        if h.wsHandler != nil && strings.EqualFold(req.Header.Get("Connection"), "upgrade") && req.Header.Get("Upgrade") == "websocket" {
    95	                h.wsHandler.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
    96	        } else {
    97	                h.handler.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
    98	        }
    99	}
   100	
   101	// Unix implementation of http.RoundTripper, required to register unix protocol in reverse proxy
   102	type unixRoundTripper struct {
   103	        Transport *http.Transport
   104	}
   105	
   106	// Implementation of https://pkg.go.dev/net/http#RoundTripper interface to support http protocol over unix socket
   107	func (t *unixRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {
   108	        // Inspired by https://github.com/tv42/httpunix
   109	        // Not having a Host, even if not used, makes the reverseproxy fail with a "no Host in request URL"
   110	        if req.Host == "" {
   111	                req.Host = "localhost"
   112	        }
   113	        req.URL.Host = req.Host
   114	        tt := t.Transport
   115	        req = req.Clone(req.Context())
   116	        req.URL.Scheme = "http"
   117	        return tt.RoundTrip(req)
   118	}
   119	
   120	// newReverseProxy creates a new reverse proxy for proxying requests to upstream
   121	// servers based on the upstream configuration provided.
   122	// The proxy should render an error page if there are failures connecting to the
   123	// upstream server.
   124	func newReverseProxy(target *url.URL, upstream options.Upstream, errorHandler ProxyErrorHandler) http.Handler {
   125	        proxy := httputil.NewSingleHostReverseProxy(target)
   126	
   127	        // Inherit default transport options from Go's stdlib
   128	        transport := http.DefaultTransport.(*http.Transport).Clone()
   129	
   130	        if target.Scheme == "unix" {
   131	                transport.DialContext = func(ctx context.Context, _, _ string) (net.Conn, error) {
   132	                        dialer := net.Dialer{}
   133	                        return dialer.DialContext(ctx, target.Scheme, target.Path)
   134	                }
   135	                transport.RegisterProtocol(target.Scheme, &unixRoundTripper{Transport: transport})
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        // Change default duration for waiting for an upstream response
   139	        if upstream.Timeout != nil {
   140	                transport.ResponseHeaderTimeout = upstream.Timeout.Duration()
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        // Configure options on the SingleHostReverseProxy
   144	        if upstream.FlushInterval != nil {
   145	                proxy.FlushInterval = upstream.FlushInterval.Duration()
   146	        } else {
   147	                proxy.FlushInterval = options.DefaultUpstreamFlushInterval
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        // InsecureSkipVerify is a configurable option we allow
   151	        /* #nosec G402 */
   152	        if upstream.InsecureSkipTLSVerify {
   153	                transport.TLSClientConfig.InsecureSkipVerify = true
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        // Ensure we always pass the original request path
   157	        setProxyDirector(proxy)
   158	
   159	        if upstream.PassHostHeader != nil && !*upstream.PassHostHeader {
   160	                setProxyUpstreamHostHeader(proxy, target)
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        // Set the error handler so that upstream connection failures render the
   164	        // error page instead of sending a empty response
   165	        if errorHandler != nil {
   166	                proxy.ErrorHandler = errorHandler
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        // Apply the customized transport to our proxy before returning it
   170	        proxy.Transport = transport
   171	
   172	        return proxy
   173	}
   174	
   175	// setProxyUpstreamHostHeader sets the proxy.Director so that upstream requests
   176	// receive a host header matching the target URL.
   177	func setProxyUpstreamHostHeader(proxy *httputil.ReverseProxy, target *url.URL) {
   178	        director := proxy.Director
   179	        proxy.Director = func(req *http.Request) {
   180	                director(req)
   181	                req.Host = target.Host
   182	        }
   183	}
   184	
   185	// setProxyDirector sets the proxy.Director so that request URIs are escaped
   186	// when proxying to usptream servers.
   187	func setProxyDirector(proxy *httputil.ReverseProxy) {
   188	        director := proxy.Director
   189	        proxy.Director = func(req *http.Request) {
   190	                director(req)
   191	                // use RequestURI so that we aren't unescaping encoded slashes in the request path
   192	                req.URL.Opaque = req.RequestURI
   193	                req.URL.RawQuery = ""
   194	                req.URL.ForceQuery = false
   195	        }
   196	}
   197	
   198	// newWebSocketReverseProxy creates a new reverse proxy for proxying websocket connections.
   199	func newWebSocketReverseProxy(u *url.URL, skipTLSVerify bool) http.Handler {
   200	        wsProxy := httputil.NewSingleHostReverseProxy(u)
   201	
   202	        // Inherit default transport options from Go's stdlib
   203	        transport := http.DefaultTransport.(*http.Transport).Clone()
   204	
   205	        /* #nosec G402 */
   206	        if skipTLSVerify {
   207	                transport.TLSClientConfig.InsecureSkipVerify = true
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        // Apply the customized transport to our proxy before returning it
   211	        wsProxy.Transport = transport
   212	
   213	        return wsProxy
   214	}

' --new_str 'func rewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, writer pagewriter.Writer, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
	return http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
		reqURL, err := url.ParseRequestURI(req.RequestURI)
		if err != nil {
			logger.Errorf("could not parse request URI: %v", err)
			writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
				Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
				RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
				AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse request URI: %v", err),
			})
			return
		}

		// Use the regex to rewrite the request path before proxying to the upstream.
		newURI := rewriteRegExp.ReplaceAllString(reqURL.Path, rewriteTarget)
		reqURL.Path, reqURL.RawQuery, err = splitPathAndQuery(reqURL.Query(), newURI)
		if err != nil {
			logger.Errorf("could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err)
			writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
				Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
				RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
				AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err),
			})
			return
		}

		if reqURL.Scheme == "" {
			req.RequestURI = reqURL.String()
		} else {
			newRequestURI := reqURL.RequestURI()
			if strings.HasPrefix(req.RequestURI, reqURL.Scheme+"://"+reqURL.Host) {
				newRequestURI = reqURL.Scheme + "://" + reqURL.Host + newRequestURI
			}
			req.RequestURI = newRequestURI
		}
		req.URL.Path = reqURL.Path // set path for websocket connections
		next.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
	})
}

    21	        }
    22	}
    23	
    24	// rewritePath uses the regexp to rewrite the request URI based on the provided
    25	// rewriteTarget.
    26	func rewritePath(rewriteRegExp *regexp.Regexp, rewriteTarget string, writer pagewriter.Writer, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
    27	return http.HandlerFunc(func(rw http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
    28	reqURL, err := url.ParseRequestURI(req.RequestURI)
    29	if err != nil {
    30	logger.Errorf("could not parse request URI: %v", err)
    31	writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
    32	Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
    33	RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
    34	AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse request URI: %v", err),
    35	})
    36	return
    37	}
    38	
    39	// Use the regex to rewrite the request path before proxying to the upstream.
    40	newURI := rewriteRegExp.ReplaceAllString(reqURL.Path, rewriteTarget)
    41	reqURL.Path, reqURL.RawQuery, err = splitPathAndQuery(reqURL.Query(), newURI)
    42	if err != nil {
    43	logger.Errorf("could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err)
    44	writer.WriteErrorPage(rw, pagewriter.ErrorPageOpts{
    45	Status:    http.StatusInternalServerError,
    46	RequestID: middleware.GetRequestScope(req).RequestID,
    47	AppError:  fmt.Sprintf("Could not parse rewrite URI: %v", err),
    48	})
    49	return
    50	}
    51	
    52	if reqURL.Scheme == "" {
    53	req.RequestURI = reqURL.String()
    54	} else {
    55	newRequestURI := reqURL.RequestURI()
    56	if strings.HasPrefix(req.RequestURI, reqURL.Scheme+"://"+reqURL.Host) {
    57	newRequestURI = reqURL.Scheme + "://" + reqURL.Host + newRequestURI
    58	}
    59	req.RequestURI = newRequestURI
    60	}
    61	req.URL.Path = reqURL.Path // set path for websocket connections
    62	next.ServeHTTP(rw, req)
    63	})
    64	}
    65	
    66	// splitPathAndQuery splits the rewritten path into the URL Path and the URL
    67	// raw query. Any rewritten query values are appended to the original query
    68	// values.
